      { type:  "box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:"rgba(68, 85, 102, 0)",stroke:"rgba(112,128,144)",width:4},
      { type: "text",position:[0,0,100,95],value:"H Middle",color:"rgba(112,128,144)"},
    ]
  };

var hit_button = {
    id:"hit_button",
    position:[1,39,13,3],
    clickable: true,
    shortcut: "B",
    visible: true,
    components: [
      { type:  "box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:"rgba(68, 85, 102, 0)",stroke:"rgba(112,128,144)",width:4},
      { type: "text",position:[0,0,100,95],value:"B Hit-Zone",color:"rgba(112,128,144)"},
    ]
  };

const gemVal = {
  1:20,
  2:80,
  3:180,
  4:320,
  5:500,
  6:720,
  7:980,
  8:1280,
};

const lastShips = [101,202,304,406,507,608];

const buttonUIs = ["hit_button","home_button","switch_button","regen_button"];

this.options = {
  root_mode: "",
  map_name: "Railgun Mod - Dueling",
  map_size: 80,
  ships: ships,
  starting_ship: 701,
  reset_tree: false,
  custom_map: [],
  max_level: 6,
  vocabulary: vocabulary,
  weapons_store: false,
  asteroids_strength: 0.5,
};

this.tick = function(game) {
  if(game.step%10===0){
    for(let ship of game.ships){
      if(ship.x>80&&ship.x<130&&ship.y<20&&ship.y>-20){
        ship.setUIComponent({
          id:"ready",
          position:[43,85,12,6],
          clickable: true,
          shortcut: "V",
          visible: true,
          components: [
            { type:  "box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:"rgba(68, 85, 102, 0)",stroke:"rgba(0, 255, 0, 1)",width:4},
            { type: "text",position:[5,5,90,90],value:"V Launch!",color:"rgba(0, 255, 0, 1)"},
          ]
        });
      }
      else{
        ship.setUIComponent({
          id:"ready",
          position:[43,85,12,6],
          clickable: false,
          shortcut: "V",
          visible: true,
          components: [
            { type:  "box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:"rgba(68, 85, 102, 0)",stroke:"rgba(255, 0, 0, 1)",width:4},
            { type: "text",position:[5,5,90,90],value:"V Launch!",color:"rgba(255, 0, 0, 1)"},
          ]
        });
      }
    }
  }
};

this.event = function(event, game) {
  switch (event.name) {
    case "ship_spawned":
    event.ship.setUIComponent(regen_button);
    event.ship.setUIComponent(switch_button);
    event.ship.setUIComponent(home_button);
    event.ship.setUIComponent(hit_button);
    event.ship.set({x:0,y:0});
      break;
    case "ui_component_clicked":
      switch (event.id) {
        case "ready":
          launch(event.ship);
          break;
          
        case "regen_button":
          regen(event.ship);
          break;
        
        case "switch_button":
          switchShip(event.ship);
          break;
        
        case "home_button":
          event.ship.set({x:0,y:0,vx:0,vy:0});
          break;
        
        case "hit_button":
          event.ship.set({x:325,y:0,vx:0,vy:0});
          break;
      }
      break;
  }
};

function launch(ship){
  ship.set({y:0,vy:0,vs:0});
  setTimeout( () => {
    ship.set({vx:speed});
  }, 500);
}

function regen(ship){
  ship.set({crystals:gemVal[Math.floor(ship.type/100).toString()],shield:ship.shield+999,stats:88888888});
}

function switchShip(ship){
  if(lastShips.includes(ship.type)){
    ship.set({type:Math.floor(ship.type/100)*100+101,stats:88888888});
  } 
  else if(ship.type>=704){
    ship.set({type:101,stats:11111111});
  }
  else{
    ship.set({type:ship.type+1,stats:88888888});
  }
}
//terminal commands
addAsteroids = function(num,size){
  for(let i=0;i<num;i++){
    game.addAsteroid({x:325,y:0,size:size});
  }
};

killAsteroids = function(){
  for(let a of game.asteroids){
    a.set({size:1,kill:true});
  }
};

shipSet = function(index,type){
  game.ships[index].set({type:type});
};

info = function(){
  for (let i=0;i<game.ships.length;i++){
    const ship = game.ships[i];
    game.modding.terminal.echo(`Index: ${i}, Name: ${ship.name}, type: ${ship.type}\nX: ${Math.round(ship.x)}, Y: ${Math.round(ship.y)}`);
  }
};

launchPlayer = function(index,speed){
  game.ships[index].set({vy:0,vx:0});
  setTimeout( () => {
    game.ships[index].set({vx:speed});
  }, 500);
};

stopPlayer = function(index,speed){
  game.ships[index].set({vy:0,vx:0});
};

stopAll = function(index,speed){
  for(let ship of game.ships){ships.set({vy:0,vx:0});}
};

runUI = function(){
  for(let ship of game.ships){
    for(let UI of buttonUIs){
      ship.setUIComponent(UI);
    }
  }
};

launchAll = function(){
  for(let i=0;i<game.ships.length;i++){
    game.ships[i].set({x:100,y:0,vy:0,vx:0});
  }
  setTimeout( () => {
    for(let i=0;i<game.ships.length;i++){
      game.ships[i].set({vx:50});
    }
  }, 500);
};
